5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Kafka @Deprecated API Migration Inventory

## Your Task

Catalog all Java source files in `apache/kafka` that contain `@Deprecated` annotations on producer/streams configuration constants or exception-handling APIs. Focus on:

1. **StreamsConfig.java** — find deprecated config constants (e.g., `CACHE_MAX_BYTES_BUFFERING_CONFIG`, `DEFAULT_DESERIALIZATION_EXCEPTION_HANDLER_CLASS_CONFIG`, `DEFAULT_PRODUCTION_EXCEPTION_HANDLER_CLASS_CONFIG`, `DEFAULT_DSL_STORE_CONFIG`) and note their replacements.
2. **Exception handler interfaces and implementations** — find deprecated `handle()` method signatures in `ProductionExceptionHandler`, `DefaultProductionExceptionHandler`, `DeserializationExceptionHandler`, `LogAndFailExceptionHandler`, and `LogAndContinueExceptionHandler`.
3. **TopicConfig.java** — find deprecated config constants (e.g., `MESSAGE_DOWNCONVERSION_ENABLE_CONFIG`).

For each file, report the repo, file path, deprecated symbol name, and what it was replaced by (if documented in the annotation or Javadoc).

## Context

You are working on a migration inventory task for the Apache Kafka ecosystem. The pinned Kafka snapshot is version 4.x — note that older deprecated producer configs like `block.on.buffer.full` and `metadata.fetch.timeout.ms` were fully removed prior to this version and will not appear.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/kafka--0753c489, sg-evals/flink--0cc95fcc, sg-evals/camel--1006f047.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/kafka--0753c489` (apache/kafka)
- `sg-evals/flink--0cc95fcc` (apache/flink)
- `sg-evals/camel--1006f047` (apache/camel)

## Output Format

Create a file at `/workspace/answer.json` with your findings in the following structure:

```json
{
  "files": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.java"}
  ],
  "symbols": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.java", "symbol": "SymbolName"}
  ],
  "chain": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.java", "symbol": "FunctionName"}
  ],
  "text": "Narrative explanation of your findings, citing repos and file paths."
}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

## Evaluation

Your answer will be scored on:
- **File recall and precision**: Did you find all relevant files?

- `DEFAULT_DSL_STORE_CONFIG`, `ROCKS_DB`, `IN_MEMORY`, `DEFAULT_DSL_STORE` → `DSL_STORE_SUPPLIERS_CLASS_CONFIG` (3.7)

### Exception Handler API Evolution (Kafka 3.9)
- `handle(ProducerRecord, Exception)` → `handle(ErrorHandlerContext, ProducerRecord, Exception)`
- `handleSerializationException(ProducerRecord, Exception)` → `handleSerializationException(ErrorHandlerContext, ProducerRecord, Exception, SerializationExceptionOrigin)`
- `handle(ProcessorContext, ConsumerRecord, Exception)` → `handle(ErrorHandlerContext, ConsumerRecord, Exception)`

instance.\n87:  * Can also be used to configure the Kafka Streams internal {@link KafkaConsumer}, {@link KafkaProducer} and {@link Admin}.\n88:  * To avoid consumer/producer/admin property conflicts, you should prefix those properties using\n89:  * {@link #consumerPrefix(String)}, {@link #producerPrefix(String)} and {@link #adminClientPrefix(String)}, respectively.\n90:  * <p>\n91:  * Example:\n92:  * <pre>{@code\n93:  * // potentially wrong: sets \"metadata.max.age.ms\" to 1 minute for producer AND consumer\n94:  * Properties streamsProperties = new Properties();\n95:  * streamsProperties.put(ConsumerConfig.METADATA_MAX_AGE_CONFIG, 60000);\n96:  * // or\n97:  * streamsProperties.put(ProducerConfig.METADATA_MAX_AGE_CONFIG, 60000);\n98:  *\n99:  * // suggested:\n100:  * Properties streamsProperties = new Properties();\n101:  * // sets \"metadata.max.age.ms\" to 1 minute for consumer only\n102:  * streamsProperties.put(StreamsConfig.consumerPrefix(ConsumerConfig.METADATA_MAX_AGE_CONFIG), 60000);\n103:  * // sets \"metadata.max.age.ms\" to 1 minute for producer only\n104:  * streamsProperties.put(StreamsConfig.producerPrefix(ProducerConfig.METADATA_MAX_AGE_CONFIG), 60000);\n105:  *\n106:  * StreamsConfig streamsConfig = new StreamsConfig(streamsProperties);\n107:  * }</pre>\n108:  *\n109:  * This instance can also be used to pass in custom configurations to different modules (e.g. passing a special config in your customized serde class).\n110:  * The consumer/producer/admin prefix can also be used to distinguish these custom config values passed to different clients with the same config name.\n111:  * * Example:\n112:  * <pre>{@code\n113:  * Properties streamsProperties = new Properties();\n114:  * // sets \"my.custom.config\" to \"foo\" for consumer only\n115:  * streamsProperties.put(StreamsConfig.consumerPrefix(\"my.custom.config\"), \"foo\");\n116:  * // sets \"my.custom.config\" to \"bar\" for producer only\n117:  * streamsProperties.put(StreamsConfig.producerPrefix(\"my.custom.config\"), \"bar\");\n118:  * // sets \"my.custom.config2\" to \"boom\" for all clients universally\n119:  * streamsProperties.put(\"my.custom.config2\", \"boom\");\n120:  *\n121:  * // as a result, inside producer's serde class configure(..) function,\n122:  * // users can now read both key-value pairs \"my.custom.config\" -> \"foo\"\n123:  * // and \"my.custom.config2\" -> \"boom\" from the config map\n124:  * StreamsConfig streamsConfig = new StreamsConfig(streamsProperties);\n125:  * }</pre>\n126:  *\n127:  *\n128:  * When increasing {@link ProducerConfig#MAX_BLOCK_MS_CONFIG} to be more resilient to non-available brokers you should also\n129:  * increase {@link ConsumerConfig#MAX_POLL_INTERVAL_MS_CONFIG} using the following guidance:\n130:  * <pre>\n131:  *     max.poll.interval.ms &gt; max.block.ms\n132:  * </pre>\n133:  *\n134:  *\n135:  * Kafka Streams requires at least the following properties to be set:\n136:  * <ul>\n137:  *  <li>{@link #APPLICATION_ID_CONFIG \"application.id\"}</li>\n138:  *  <li>{@link #BOOTSTRAP_SERVERS_CONFIG \"bootstrap.servers\"}</li>\n139:  * </ul>\n140:  *\n141:  * By default, Kafka Streams does not allow users to overwrite the following properties (Streams setting shown in parentheses):\n142:  * <ul>\n143:  *   <li>{@link ConsumerConfig#GROUP_ID_CONFIG \"group.id\"} (&lt;application.id&gt;) - Streams client will always use the application ID a consumer group ID</li>\n144:  *   <li>{@link ConsumerConfig#ENABLE_AUTO_COMMIT_CONFIG \"enable.auto.commit\"} (false) - Streams client will always disable/turn off auto committing</li>\n145:  *   <li>{@link ConsumerConfig#PARTITION_ASSIGNMENT_STRATEGY_CONFIG \"partition.assignment.strategy\"} (<code>StreamsPartitionAssignor</code>) - Streams client will always use its own partition assignor</li>\n146:  * </ul>\n147:  *\n148:  * If {@link #PROCESSING_GUARANTEE_CONFIG \"processing.guarantee\"} is set to {@link #EXACTLY_ONCE_V2 \"exactly_once_v2\"},\n149:  * Kafka Streams does not allow users to overwrite the following properties (Streams setting shown in parentheses):\n150:  * <ul>\n151:  *   <li>{@link ConsumerConfig#ISOLATION_LEVEL_CONFIG \"isolation.level\"} (read_committed) - Consumers will always read committed data only</li>\n152:  *   <li>{@link ProducerConfig#ENABLE_IDEMPOTENCE_CONFIG \"enable.idempotence\"} (true) - Producer will always have idempotency enabled</li>\n153:  * </ul>\n154:  *\n155:  * @see KafkaStreams#KafkaStreams(org.apache.kafka.streams.Topology, Properties)\n156:  * @see ConsumerConfig\n157:  * @see ProducerConfig\n158:  */\n159: public class instance.\\n87:  * Can also be used to configure the Kafka Streams internal {@link KafkaConsumer}, {@link KafkaProducer} and {@link Admin}.\\n88:  * To avoid consumer/producer/admin property conflicts, you should prefix those properties using\\n89:  * {@link #consumerPrefix(String)}, {@link #producerPrefix(String)} and {@link #adminClientPrefix(String)}, respectively.\\n90:  * <p>\\n91:  * Example:\\n92:  * <pre>{@code\\n93:  * // potentially wrong: sets \\\"metadata.max.age.ms\\\" to 1 minute for producer AND consumer\\n94:  * Properties streamsProperties = new Properties();\\n95:  * streamsProperties.put(ConsumerConfig.METADATA_MAX_AGE_CONFIG, 60000);\\n96:  * // or\\n97:  * streamsProperties.put(ProducerConfig.METADATA_MAX_AGE_CONFIG, 60000);\\n98:  *\\n99:  * // suggested:\\n100:  * Properties streamsProperties = new Properties();\\n101:  * // sets \\\"metadata.max.age.ms\\\" to 1 minute for consumer only\\n102:  * streamsProperties.put(StreamsConfig.consumerPrefix(ConsumerConfig.METADATA_MAX_AGE_CONFIG), 60000);\\n103:  * // sets \\\"metadata.max.age.ms\\\" to 1 minute for producer only\\n104:  * streamsProperties.put(StreamsConfig.producerPrefix(ProducerConfig.METADATA_MAX_AGE_CONFIG), 60000);\\n105:  *\\n106:  * StreamsConfig streamsConfig = new StreamsConfig(streamsProperties);\\n107:  * }</pre>\\n108:  *\\n109:  * This instance can also be used to pass in custom configurations to different modules (e.g. passing a special config in your customized serde class).\\n110:  * The consumer/producer/admin prefix can also be used to distinguish these custom config values passed to different clients with the same config name.\\n111:  * * Example:\\n112:  * <pre>{@code\\n113:  * Properties streamsProperties = new Properties();\\n114:  * // sets \\\"my.custom.config\\\" to \\\"foo\\\" for consumer only\\n115:  * streamsProperties.put(StreamsConfig.consumerPrefix(\\\"my.custom.config\\\"), \\\"foo\\\");\\n116:  * // sets \\\"my.custom.config\\\" to \\\"bar\\\" for producer only\\n117:  * streamsProperties.put(StreamsConfig.producerPrefix(\\\"my.custom.config\\\"), \\\"bar\\\");\\n118:  * // sets \\\"my.custom.config2\\\" to \\\"boom\\\" for all clients universally\\n119:  * streamsProperties.put(\\\"my.custom.config2\\\", \\\"boom\\\");\\n120:  *\\n121:  * // as a result, inside producer's serde class configure(..) function,\\n122:  * // users can now read both key-value pairs \\\"my.custom.config\\\" -> \\\"foo\\\"\\n123:  * // and \\\"my.custom.config2\\\" -> \\\"boom\\\" from the config map\\n124:  * StreamsConfig streamsConfig = new StreamsConfig(streamsProperties);\\n125:  * }</pre>\\n126:  *\\n127:  *\\n128:  * When increasing {@link ProducerConfig#MAX_BLOCK_MS_CONFIG} to be more resilient to non-available brokers you should also\\n129:  * increase {@link ConsumerConfig#MAX_POLL_INTERVAL_MS_CONFIG} using the following guidance:\\n130:  * <pre>\\n131:  *     max.poll.interval.ms &gt; max.block.ms\\n132:  * </pre>\\n133:  *\\n134:  *\\n135:  * Kafka Streams requires at least the following properties to be set:\\n136:  * <ul>\\n137:  *  <li>{@link #APPLICATION_ID_CONFIG \\\"application.id\\\"}</li>\\n138:  *  <li>{@link #BOOTSTRAP_SERVERS_CONFIG \\\"bootstrap.servers\\\"}</li>\\n139:  * </ul>\\n140:  *\\n141:  * By default, Kafka Streams does not allow users to overwrite the following properties (Streams setting shown in parentheses):\\n142:  * <ul>\\n143:  *   <li>{@link ConsumerConfig#GROUP_ID_CONFIG \\\"group.id\\\"} (&lt;application.id&gt;) - Streams client will always use the application ID a consumer group ID</li>\\n144:  *   <li>{@link ConsumerConfig#ENABLE_AUTO_COMMIT_CONFIG \\\"enable.auto.commit\\\"} (false) - Streams client will always disable/turn off auto committing</li>\\n145:  *   <li>{@link ConsumerConfig#PARTITION_ASSIGNMENT_STRATEGY_CONFIG \\\"partition.assignment.strategy\\\"} (<code>StreamsPartitionAssignor</code>) - Streams client will always use its own partition assignor</li>\\n146:  * </ul>\\n147:  *\\n148:  * If {@link #PROCESSING_GUARANTEE_CONFIG \\\"processing.guarantee\\\"} is set to {@link #EXACTLY_ONCE_V2 \\\"exactly_once_v2\\\"},\\n149:  * Kafka Streams does not allow users to overwrite the following properties (Streams setting shown in parentheses):\\n150:  * <ul>\\n151:  *   <li>{@link ConsumerConfig#ISOLATION_LEVEL_CONFIG \\\"isolation.level\\\"} (read_committed) - Consumers will always read committed data only</li>\\n152:  *   <li>{@link ProducerConfig#ENABLE_IDEMPOTENCE_CONFIG \\\"enable.idempotence\\\"} (true) - import json
import sys

data = json.load(sys.stdin)
content = data['content']
lines = content.split('\n')

# Find all @Deprecated annotations and their context
deprecated_items = []
i = 0
while i < len(lines):
    if '@Deprecated' in lines[i]:
        # Collect context
        start = max(0, i - 2)
        end = min(len(lines), i + 10)
        context = '\n'.join(lines[start:end])
        deprecated_items.append(context)
        print(f"=== ITEM {len(deprecated_items)} ===")
        print(context)
        print()
        i = end
    else:
        i += 1
EOF

8. $ python3 << 'EOF'
import json
import re

with open('/logs/agent/sessions/projects/-workspace/5f082281-2dc5-4ff9-bcf0-d64eade8666a/tool-results/mcp-sourcegraph-sg_read_file-1772143971929.txt', 'r') as f:
    data = json.load(f)
    lines = data['content'].split('\n')

# Find @Deprecated and extract symbol names and replacements
deprecated_symbols = []
for i, line in enumerate(lines):
    if '@Deprecated' in line:
        # Get surrounding lines for context
        start = max(0, i - 10)
        end = min(len(lines), i + 5)
        context = '\n'.join(lines[start:end])
        
        # Extract the symbol name (usually the next public static final after @Deprecated)
        symbol_match = re.search(r'public static final.*?\s+(\w+)\s*=', context)
        
        # Extract javadoc comment with @deprecated
        javadoc_match = re.search(r'@deprecated\s+([^*]+?)(?:\*\/|@)', context, re.DOTALL)
        replacement = javadoc_match.group(1).strip() if javadoc_match else None
        
        if symbol_match:
            symbol = symbol_match.group(1)
            deprecated_symbols.append({
                'line': i + 1,
                'symbol': symbol,
                'replacement': replacement
            })

# Print all
for item in deprecated_symbols:
    print(f"Line {item['line']}: {item['symbol']}")
    if item['replacement']:
        print(f"  → {item['replacement']}")
    print()
EOF

import json

    lines = data['content'].split('\n')

# Find all @Deprecated lines and their context
deprecated_items = []
for i, line in enumerate(lines):
    if '@Deprecated' in line:
        # Get surrounding lines for context (more lines for better extraction)
        start = max(0, i - 15)
        end = min(len(lines), i + 10)
        context_lines = lines[start:end]
        
        deprecated_items.append({
            'line': i + 1,
            'context_start': start + 1,
            'context': '\n'.join(context_lines)
        })

# Print first 10 for manual inspection
print(f"Total @Deprecated annotations: {len(deprecated_items)}\n")
for j, item in enumerate(deprecated_items[:15]):
    print(f"=== ITEM {j+1} (Line {item['line']}) ===")
    for idx, line in enumerate(item['context'].split('\n'), item['context_start']):
        print(f"{idx}: {line}")
    print()
EOF

10. $ python3 << 'EOF'
import json
import re

with open('/logs/agent/sessions/projects/-workspace/5f082281-2dc5-4ff9-bcf0-d64eade8666a/tool-results/mcp-sourcegraph-sg_read_file-1772143971929.txt', 'r') as f:
    data = json.load(f)
    lines = data['content'].split('\n')

# Find @Deprecated and extract symbol names and replacements
deprecated_symbols = []
for i, line in enumerate(lines):
    if '@Deprecated' in line:
        # Look back for javadoc with @deprecated info
        deprecation_message = ""
        for j in range(i - 1, max(-1, i - 20), -1):
            if '@deprecated' in lines[j]:
                # Extract the deprecation message
                deprecation_message = lines[j]
                break
        
        # Look forward for the public static final declaration
        symbol_name = ""
        for j in range(i + 1, min(len(lines), i + 10)):
            public_match = re.search(r'public static final\s+\w+\s+(\w+)\s*=', lines[j])
            if public_match:
                symbol_name = public_match.group(1)
                break
        
        if symbol_name:
            deprecated_symbols.append({
                'line': i + 1,
                'symbol': symbol_name,
                'deprecation_msg': deprecation_message.strip()
            })

# Print all
print(f"Total deprecated symbols found: {len(deprecated_symbols)}\n")
for item in deprecated_symbols:
    print(f"Line {item['line']:4d}: {item['symbol']:50s} | {item['deprecation_msg']}")
EOF
